ANALYSIS
================================================================================

Baseline (clean): 69.04% token accuracy

Impact of individual noise types:
  Dropout (15%):       Δ=+21.50%
  Noise peaks (10):    Δ=+21.19%
  Mass error (15ppm):  Δ=+1.60%
  ALL combined:        Δ=+32.33%

🔴 Worst offender: Dropout (Δ=21.50%)
   This noise type has the largest negative impact on accuracy

Charge state comparison:
  +2 (clean): 69.59%
  +3 (clean): 68.35%
  Difference: +1.24%
  ✅ Model handles both charge states equally

================================================================================
INTERPRETATION & RECOMMENDATIONS
================================================================================

1. DROPOUT is the main challenge
   Recommendation:
   - Increase dropout during training (train harder)
   - Consider adding attention to precursor mass (global constraint)
   - Longer peptides suffer more from dropout (fewer peaks)

Noise interaction effect:
  Expected (additive): 44.29%
  Actual (combined):   32.33%
  Synergy:             -11.95%
  ✅ SUBADDITIVE: Some noise types overlap
     Model partially robust to combined noise
